Abstract: In process operations, it is desirable to manage the sensitivity of the system output against external disturbance in the form of finite $\mathcal{L}_2$-gain stabilization. This matter is, however, nonsensical for stochastic systems because the stochastic uncertainties in the control input almost always lead to an unbounded $\mathcal{L}_2$ gain from the disturbance to the output. To address this issue, this article develops a novel concept that characterizes the $\mathcal{L}_2$ gain of stochastic systems in a probabilistic way. Combined with a large data set, we formulate a data-driven probabilistic finite $\mathcal{L}_2$-gain stabilization design using noisy trajectory measurements and the disturbance forecast that does not necessarily agree with the actual future disturbance. ### [254] [Homotopy-Guided Potential Games for Congestion-Aware Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13708)
*Mohammed Irshadh Ismaaeel Sathyamangalam Imran,Lasse Peters,Michael Khayyat,Stefano Arrigoni,Francesco Braghin,Laura Ferranti*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 提出统一框架结合同伦规划和博弈论，解决多智能体运动规划中的交互、碰撞和拥堵问题，通过同伦类作为策略集，在滚动时域中寻找广义开环纳什均衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统博弈论规划器能捕捉智能体交互但往往收敛到保守、拥堵的均衡解；同伦规划器能探索拓扑不同的路径但缺乏考虑智能体未来动作的相互依赖性。需要统一框架同时解决交互、碰撞和拥堵问题。

Method: 1) 在滚动时域框架下，将同伦类作为结构化策略集；2) 确定性同伦规划器为每个智能体生成拓扑不同的路径；3) 使用启发式过滤选择top-K无拥堵联合策略；4) 构建势博弈，施加同伦一致性约束，获得广义开环纳什均衡，惩罚滚动时域中的策略突变。

Abstract: We address the multi-agent motion planning problem where interactions, collisions, and congestion co-exist. Conventional game-theoretic planners capture interactions among agents but often converge to conservative, congested equilibria. Homotopy planners, on the other hand, can explore topologically distinct paths, but lack mechanisms to account for the interdependence of agents' future actions. We propose a unified framework that leverages homotopy classes as structured strategy sets within a receding-horizon setup. At each planning stage, a deterministic homotopy planner generates topologically distinct paths for each agent, conditioned on the joint configuration. To avoid intractable growth of candidate paths, we propose a simple heuristic filtering step that selects a top-$K$ subset of the most suitable congestion-free joint strategies to ensure computational tractability. These serve as initializations for a potential game that enforces homotopy-consistent constraints and yields a generalized open-loop Nash equilibrium (OLNE), with penalties discouraging abrupt strategy shifts in a receding-horizon setting. Simulations with three agents demonstrate improved efficiency (faster completion) and enhanced safety (greater inter-agent clearance, leading to reduced congestion) compared to a local baseline and NH-ORCA that do not reason about homotopies. Hardware trials with two robots and one human demonstrate robustness to irrational behaviors, where our method adapts by switching to alternative feasible equilibria while the baseline game fails.

</details>


### [255] [A Dynamic-Growing Fuzzy-Neuro Controller, Application to a 3PSP Parallel Robot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13763)
*Mohsen Jalaeian-Farimani,Mohammad-R Akbarzadeh-T,Alireza Akbarzadeh,Mostafa Ghaemi*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 提出一种结合动态增长模糊神经控制器(DGFNC)与自适应策略的3PSP并联机器人位置控制方法，通过保守的规则增长机制和滑动模态控制确保系统稳定性，实现快速响应和低计算量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软计算范式在解决现代问题中具有广泛应用，其中模糊系统与神经网络的自主组织组合能够构建强大的决策系统。3PSP并联机器人因其复杂的动力学特性以及在现代工业系统中的实用性，成为验证此类方法的理想平台。

Method: 采用动态增长模糊神经控制器(DGFNC)结合自适应策略，其中DGFNC采用保守的规则增长机制（省略剪枝机制），自适应策略应对参数变化，同时使用基于滑动模态的非线性控制器确保系统稳定性。

Result: 通过多个仿真验证，所提出的DGFNC策略在3PSP机器人控制中表现出优越性能，实现了更快的响应速度和更少的计算量，同时保持了整体系统的稳定性。

Conclusion: DGFNC结合自适应策略为复杂机器人系统提供了一种有效的控制方案，通过保守的规则增长和滑动模态控制，在保证稳定性的前提下实现了计算效率和响应速度的优化。

Abstract: To date, various paradigms of soft-Computing have been used to solve many modern problems. Among them, a self organizing combination of fuzzy systems and neural networks can make a powerful decision making system. Here, a Dynamic Growing Fuzzy Neural Controller (DGFNC) is combined with an adaptive strategy and applied to a 3PSP parallel robot position control problem. Specifically, the dynamic growing mechanism is considered in more detail. In contrast to other self-organizing methods, DGFNC adds new rules more conservatively; hence the pruning mechanism is omitted. Instead, the adaptive strategy 'adapts' the control system to parameter variation. Furthermore, a sliding mode-based nonlinear controller ensures system stability. The resulting general control strategy aims to achieve faster response with less computation while maintaining overall stability. Finally, the 3PSP is chosen due to its complex dynamics and the utility of such approaches in modern industrial systems. Several simulations support the merits of the proposed DGFNC strategy as applied to the 3PSP robot.

### [256] [Importance of Aggregated DER Installed Capacity in Distribution Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13926)
*Alexandre M. V. Gouveia,Md. Umar Hashmi,Reinhilde D'hulst,Dirk Van Hertem*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 提出一种基于变电站和馈线测量数据估算低压聚合点分布式能源装机容量的方法，以解决配电网运营商缺乏DER容量准确信息的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分布式能源（特别是电动汽车、热泵和光伏系统）在低压配电网中的渗透率不断提高，但配电网运营商缺乏对低压变电站下游DER容量的可靠和最新了解。有限的观测能力、不完整的拓扑信息和受限的客户级数据访问使得难以维护准确的DER注册表，给运行和规划过程带来不确定性。

Method: 提出在低压聚合点估算DER装机容量的聚合方法，利用常见的变电站和馈线测量数据进行估算，避免需要客户级监控。将估算结果与运行和规划需求联系起来。

Result: 该方法提供了一种实用且可扩展的方法来提高DER意识，支持DER感知预测、拥塞管理、灵活性量化、承载能力评估和DER采用监控等应用。

Conclusion: 聚合DER装机容量估算为配电网运营商提供了一种无需客户级监控的实用解决方案，能够显著改善对DER的认知，支持更有效的运行和规划决策。

Abstract: The increasing penetration of Distributed Energy Resources (DERs), particularly electric vehicles, heat pumps, and photovoltaic systems, is fundamentally changing power flows in Low-Voltage (LV) distribution networks. Despite this transition, Distribution System Operators (DSOs) often lack reliable and up-to-date knowledge of the DER capacity connected downstream of LV substations. Limited observability, incomplete topology information, and restricted access to customer-level data make it difficult to maintain accurate DER registries, creating uncertainty in both operational and planning processes. This paper presents aggregated DER installed capacity, estimated at LV aggregation points, as a practical and scalable approach to improving DER awareness without requiring customer-level monitoring. We define the problem of estimating DER installed capacities from commonly available substation and feeder measurements. By linking these estimates to operational and planning needs, we discuss how knowledge of aggregated DER installed capacity enhances DER-aware forecasting, congestion management, flexibility quantification, hosting capacity assessment, and monitoring of DER adoption.

### [257] [Joint Identification of Linear Dynamics and Noise Covariance via Distributional Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14130)
*Yang Hu,Na Li*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 提出一个联合识别线性系统动力学和噪声协方差的新框架，适用于高斯以外的噪声分布，通过最大似然估计和分数匹配估计提高识别精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法通常假设高斯噪声，但在实际应用中噪声分布可能更复杂。需要同时估计系统动力学矩阵和噪声协方差矩阵，以更准确地建模系统行为。

Method: 1. 提出状态转移分布的新参数化方法，更好地利用分布"形状"信息；2. 引入两种估计器：最大似然估计(MLE)和分数匹配估计(SME)；3. 提供统计性质和样本复杂度的严格分析。

Result: 仿真结果表明，提出的估计器在识别精度上优于普通最小二乘(OLS)基线方法。

Conclusion: 该框架能够有效处理非高斯噪声分布，通过联合识别系统动力学和噪声协方差，提高了线性系统识别的准确性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a novel framework for the joint identification of system dynamics and noise covariance in linear systems, under general noise distributions beyond Gaussian. Specifically, we would like to simultaneously estimate the dynamical matrix $A$ and the noise covariance matrix $\varSigma$ using state transition data. The formulation builds upon a novel parameterization of the state-transition distribution, which enables more effective use of distributional "shape" information for improved identification accuracy. We introduce two practical estimators, namely the maximum likelihood estimator (MLE) and the score-matching estimator (SME), to solve the joint dynamics-covariance identification problem, and provide rigorous analysis of their statistical properties and sample complexity. Simulation results show that the proposed estimators outperform the ordinary least squares (OLS) baseline.

</details>
